Railway BLW Apprentices Vacancy 2025 Online Form
üîó ‚Ä¢ Banaras Locomotive Works (BLW), Indian Railways, has released the official notification for the 47th Batch Act Apprentice Recruitment 2025. A total of 374 apprentice posts are available for both ITI and Non-ITI candidates. The trades include Fitter (137 posts), Carpenter (3), Painter (General) (7), Machinist (82), Welder (G&E) (56), and Electrician (89). For ITI posts, candidates must have passed Class 10th with at least 50% marks and hold an ITI certificate in the relevant trade from NCVT/SCVT. For Non-ITI posts, only 10th pass with 50% marks is required. The application process is completely online through the official website blw.indianrailways.gov.in. Interested candidates must apply before the last date as mentioned in the notification.
RSSB Lab Attendant Vacancy 2025 Online Form
üîó ‚Ä¢ The Rajasthan Staff Selection Board (RSSB) has released the notification for Lab Attendant (Prayogshala Sahayak) Recruitment 2025. Eligible candidates can apply online through the official website. This recruitment is a great opportunity for 10th pass candidates seeking government jobs in Rajasthan. Applicants must have a valid domicile of Rajasthan to claim reservation benefits; candidates from other states can apply under the unreserved category (UR). The selection process will include a written examination followed by document verification. Interested candidates are advised to read the official notification carefully and apply before the last date.

Indian Army SSC Tech Vacancy 2025 Online Form
üîó ‚Ä¢ The Indian Army has released the short notification for SSC Technical Entry 66th Course for Men and Women. A total of 379 vacancies are available, including 350 for men and 29 for women. The course will commence in April 2026 at Officers Training Academy (OTA), Chennai. Candidates with a Degree in Engineering (B.E. / B.Tech) in relevant disciplines are eligible to apply. The online application process will begin on 16 July 2025 and continue until 14 August 2025 through the official website joinindianarmy.nic.in. This is a great opportunity for aspiring engineers to join the Indian Army as Short Service Commission Officers.

BPSC Lower Division Clerk LDC Vacancy 2025 Online Form
üîó ‚Ä¢ The Bihar Public Service Commission (BPSC) has released a notification for the recruitment of Lower Division Clerk (LDC) posts with a total of 26 vacancies. Candidates who have passed Intermediate (10+2) in any stream from a recognized board and possess computer operation and typing skills are eligible to apply. This recruitment is primarily for domicile candidates of Bihar, who will receive reservation benefits as per their category. Candidates from other states can also apply but will be considered under the General (Unreserved) category only, without any reservation or age relaxation. The application process is completely online. Out of the total posts, 13 are for General, 3 for EWS, 4 for SC, 1 for ST, 2 for EBC, 2 for BC, and 1 for BC Female.

Bihar Home Guard Recruitment 2025

Short Details of Notification Bihar HG Advt No. : 01/2025

Important Dates

  • Application Begin: 27/03/2025

  • Exam Date: 30/04/2025 to 05/06/2025
  • Admit Card Available: 24/04/2025
  • Result Available: 04/07/2025

Application Fee

  • General / OBC / EWS: 200/-
  • SC / ST: 100/-
  • All Category Female: 100/-

  • Age Limit as on 01/01/2025

  • Minimum Age: 19 Years.
  • Maximum Age: 40 Years.

CG Abkari Aarakshak Bharti 2025 Online Form
üîó ‚Ä¢ CG Abkari Aarakshak Bharti 2025 invites applications for 200 Excise Constable posts. Eligible candidates who have passed 12th can apply online from June 4 to June 27, 2025. The written exam will be held on July 27, 2025. Applicants from all Indian states can apply, but only Chhattisgarh residents will receive reservation and age relaxation benefits. The recruitment will be conducted by CG Vyapam, and the selection process includes a written test and physical eligibility test.

NTA Common University Admission Test CUET UG 2025

National Testing Agency (NTA)

Short Details of Notification NTA CUET UG Exam 2025

Important Dates

  • Application Begin : 01/03/2025
  • Last Date for Apply Online : 24/03/2025
  • Last Date Online Payment : 25/03/2025
  • Correction Date : 26-28 March 2025
  • NTA CUET UG 2025 Exam Start : 13/05/2025
  • Exam City Available : 07/05/2025
  • Admit Card Available : Before Exam
  • Result Declared : Notified Soon

Application Fee

  • General: 1000/-
  • EWS / OBC: 900/-
  • SC / ST / PH: 800/-
  • Additional Subject Charge:
  • General: 400/- Each Subject
  • EWS / OBC: 375/- Each Subject
  • SC / ST / PH: 350/- Each Subject

  • Pay the Examination Fee Through E Challan Offline Mode or Pay the Exam Fee Through Online Debit Card, Credit Card or Net Banking Fee Mode

Eligibility

  • CUET UG Notification 2025: Age Limit

  • No Age Limit in Common University Entrance Test CUET UG 2025

Age relaxation as per rules of NTA CUET UG Exam 2025.

RSSB Rajasthan NHM (Contractual Posts) 2025 Recruitment

Rajasthan Staff Selection Board (RSSB) | RSMSSB

Short Details of Notification RSSB NHM Advt No. : 01/2025

Important Dates

  • Application Begin: 02/04/2025
  • Last Date for Apply Online: 01/05/2025
  • Pay Exam Fee Last Date: 01/05/2025
  • RSSB NHM Exam Date: As per Schedule
  • Admit Card Available: Before Exam

Application Fee

  • General / OBC: 600/-
  • OBC NCL: 400/-
  • SC / ST: 400/-
  • Correction Charge: 300/-

  • This fee is for one time registration, now after paying the OTR fee once, the candidate will not have to pay the application fee again and again.

  • Pay the Exam Fee Through Emitra CSC Center, Debit Card, Credit Card, Net Banking.

Eligibility

  • Age Limit as on 01/01/2026

  • Minimum Age: 21 Years
  • Maximum Age: 40 Years

Age relaxation as per rules of RSSB NHM Advt No. : 01/2025.

üì¢ ‡§≠‡§æ‡§∞‡§§ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§π‡§ø‡§Ç‡§¶‡•Ç ‡§ß‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§è‡§ï ‡§Æ‡§π‡§§‡•ç‡§µ‡§™‡•Ç‡§∞‡•ç‡§£ ‡§§‡•Ä‡§∞‡•ç‡§• ‡§Ø‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§ú‡§ø‡§∏‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ö‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ñ ‡§ß‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§∂‡§æ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§≤ ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç:

  • ‡§Ø‡§Æ‡•Å‡§®‡•ã‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä (‡§â‡§§‡•ç‡§§‡§∞‡§æ‡§ñ‡§Ç‡§°) ‚Äì ‡§Ø‡§Æ‡•Å‡§®‡§æ ‡§®‡§¶‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§â‡§¶‡•ç‡§ó‡§Æ ‡§∏‡•ç‡§•‡§≤

  • ‡§â‡§ö‡•ç‡§ö ‡§∞‡§ï‡•ç‡§§‡§ö‡§æ‡§™, ‡§Ö‡§∏‡•ç‡§•‡§Æ‡§æ, ‡§π‡•É‡§¶‡§Ø ‡§∞‡•ã‡§ó ‡§ú‡•à‡§∏‡•Ä ‡§∏‡§Æ‡§∏‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ì‡§Ç ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ó‡•ç‡§∞‡§∏‡§ø‡§§ ‡§≤‡•ã‡§ó‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§°‡•â‡§ï‡•ç‡§ü‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§∏‡§≤‡§æ‡§π ‡§≤‡•á‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§¨‡§æ‡§¶ ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§Ø‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•Ä ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è‡•§

  • ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü ‡§∏‡§æ‡§á‡§ú ‡§´‡•ã‡§ü‡•ã

  • ‡§ï‡•ã‡§µ‡§ø‡§° ‡§µ‡•à‡§ï‡•ç‡§∏‡§ø‡§®‡•á‡§∂‡§® ‡§∏‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü‡§ø‡§´‡§ø‡§ï‡•á‡§ü (‡§Ø‡§¶‡§ø ‡§Ü‡§µ‡§∂‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï ‡§π‡•ã)
üì¢ ‡§µ‡§ø‡§∂‡•á‡§∑ ‡§µ‡§∞‡•ç‡§ó ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§õ‡•Ç‡§ü:
  • ‡§µ‡§∞‡§ø‡§∑‡•ç‡§† ‡§®‡§æ‡§ó‡§∞‡§ø‡§ï‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§¶‡§ø‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ó ‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§§‡§ø‡§Ø‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§µ‡§ø‡§∂‡•á‡§∑ ‡§∏‡•Å‡§µ‡§ø‡§ß‡§æ‡§è‡§Å ‡§â‡§™‡§≤‡§¨‡•ç‡§ß ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§
  • ‡§Æ‡§π‡§ø‡§≤‡§æ ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§¨‡•Å‡§ú‡•Å‡§∞‡•ç‡§ó‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§π‡•á‡§≤‡•ç‡§™‡§≤‡§æ‡§á‡§® ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§°‡§ø‡§ï‡§≤ ‡§∏‡§π‡§æ‡§Ø‡§§‡§æ ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§â‡§™‡§≤‡§¨‡•ç‡§ß ‡§π‡•à‡•§
üì¢ üåü ‡§ö‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ß‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§®‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§â‡§®‡§ï‡§æ ‡§Æ‡§π‡§§‡•ç‡§µ:

üì¢ ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü (Passport) ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç ?
  • ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü ‡§è‡§ï ‡§∏‡§∞‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§¶‡§∏‡•ç‡§§‡§æ‡§µ‡•á‡§ú‡§º ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§ú‡§ø‡§∏‡•á ‡§¶‡•á‡§∂ ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§∏‡§∞‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§®‡§æ‡§ó‡§∞‡§ø‡§ï‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§è‡§ï ‡§™‡§π‡§ö‡§æ‡§® ‡§™‡§§‡•ç‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∞‡•Ç‡§™ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§á‡§∏‡•á ‡§Ö‡§Ç‡§§‡§∞‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§∑‡•ç‡§ü‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä‡§Ø ‡§Ø‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§Ü‡§µ‡§∂‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ß‡§æ‡§∞‡§ï ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§®‡§æ‡§Æ, ‡§´‡•ã‡§ü‡•ã, ‡§ú‡§®‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§§‡§ø‡§•‡§ø, ‡§™‡§§‡§æ, ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§®‡§æ‡§ó‡§∞‡§ø‡§ï‡§§‡§æ ‡§ú‡•à‡§∏‡•Ä ‡§Æ‡§π‡§§‡•ç‡§µ‡§™‡•Ç‡§∞‡•ç‡§£ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Å ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§
üì¢ üìú ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü ‡§ï‡•á ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞
  • ‡§≠‡§æ‡§∞‡§§ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§§‡•Ä‡§® ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü ‡§ú‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§ø‡§è ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç:
  • ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü
  • ‡§Ü‡§ß‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡§ø‡§ï ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü
  • ‡§ï‡•Ç‡§ü‡§®‡•Ä‡§§‡§ø‡§ï ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü
üì¢ ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü (Ordinary Passport - Type P):
  • ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§Ü‡§Æ ‡§®‡§æ‡§ó‡§∞‡§ø‡§ï‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§ú‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
  • ‡§á‡§∏‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ï‡§µ‡§∞ ‡§®‡•Ä‡§≤‡•á ‡§∞‡§Ç‡§ó ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
üì¢ ‡§Ü‡§ß‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡§ø‡§ï ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü (Official Passport - Type S):
  • ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§∏‡§∞‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§Ö‡§ß‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡§ø‡§Ø‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∏‡§∞‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§ú‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
  • ‡§á‡§∏‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ï‡§µ‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§´‡•á‡§¶ ‡§∞‡§Ç‡§ó ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
üì¢ ‡§ï‡•Ç‡§ü‡§®‡•Ä‡§§‡§ø‡§ï ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü (Diplomatic Passport - Type D):
  • ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§∞‡§æ‡§ú‡§®‡§Ø‡§ø‡§ï‡•ã‡§Ç, ‡§∏‡§∞‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§â‡§ö‡•ç‡§ö ‡§Ö‡§ß‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡§ø‡§Ø‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Ö‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§µ‡§ø‡§∂‡•á‡§∑ ‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§§‡§ø‡§Ø‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
  • ‡§á‡§∏‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ï‡§µ‡§∞ ‡§ó‡§π‡§∞‡•á ‡§≤‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§∞‡§Ç‡§ó ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
üì¢ üåç ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§æ‡§≠
  • ‡§µ‡§ø‡§¶‡•á‡§∂ ‡§Ø‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§Ü‡§µ‡§∂‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï: ‡§Ö‡§Ç‡§§‡§∞‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§∑‡•ç‡§ü‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä‡§Ø ‡§Ø‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü ‡§Ö‡§®‡§ø‡§µ‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
  • ‡§µ‡•à‡§∂‡•ç‡§µ‡§ø‡§ï ‡§™‡§π‡§ö‡§æ‡§®: ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü ‡§ß‡§æ‡§∞‡§ï ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§™‡§π‡§ö‡§æ‡§® ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§Ö‡§Ç‡§§‡§∞‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§∑‡•ç‡§ü‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä‡§Ø ‡§∏‡•ç‡§§‡§∞ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø‡§§‡§æ ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§≤‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§
  • ‡§µ‡•Ä‡§ú‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§µ‡•á‡§¶‡§® ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§∏‡§π‡•Ç‡§≤‡§ø‡§Ø‡§§: ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü ‡§π‡•ã‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡•á ‡§Ö‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§¶‡•á‡§∂‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•á ‡§µ‡•Ä‡§ú‡§æ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§Ü‡§µ‡•á‡§¶‡§® ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§∏‡§æ‡§® ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
  • ‡§¨‡•à‡§Ç‡§ï ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§™‡§π‡§ö‡§æ‡§® ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∞‡•Ç‡§™ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§â‡§™‡§Ø‡•ã‡§ó: ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§â‡§™‡§Ø‡•ã‡§ó ‡§™‡§π‡§ö‡§æ‡§® ‡§™‡§§‡•ç‡§∞ (ID Proof) ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∞‡•Ç‡§™ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ ‡§∏‡§ï‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

  • ‡§™‡•à‡§® ‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§° (PAN Card) ‡§è‡§ï ‡§∏‡•ç‡§•‡§æ‡§Ø‡•Ä ‡§ñ‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§ñ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ (Permanent Account Number) ‡§π‡•à, ‡§ú‡•ã ‡§≠‡§æ‡§∞‡§§ ‡§∏‡§∞‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§Ü‡§Ø‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§µ‡§ø‡§≠‡§æ‡§ó (Income Tax Department) ‡§¶‡•ç‡§µ‡§æ‡§∞‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§è‡§ï 10 ‡§Ö‡§Ç‡§ï‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§Ö‡§≤‡•ç‡§´‡§æ‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø‡•Ç‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡§ø‡§ï ‡§®‡§Ç‡§¨‡§∞ ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§ú‡•ã ‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§§‡§ø, ‡§´‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ï‡§Ç‡§™‡§®‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§è‡§ï ‡§µ‡§ø‡§∂‡§ø‡§∑‡•ç‡§ü ‡§™‡§π‡§ö‡§æ‡§® ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§ñ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∞‡•Ç‡§™ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§™‡•à‡§® ‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§° ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§â‡§™‡§Ø‡•ã‡§ó ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ñ‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§∞‡•Ç‡§™ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§µ‡§ø‡§§‡•ç‡§§‡•Ä‡§Ø ‡§≤‡•á‡§®-‡§¶‡•á‡§® ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§≠‡•Å‡§ó‡§§‡§æ‡§® ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

How to Self-Link DBT with NPCI? ‚Äì Easy Online & Offline Methods

üì¢ NPCI ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§π‡•à ‡§§‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ï‡•á‡•§
  • NPCI (‡§®‡•á‡§∂‡§®‡§≤ ‡§™‡•á‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç‡§ü‡•ç‡§∏ ‡§ï‡•â‡§∞‡§™‡•ã‡§∞‡•á‡§∂‡§® ‡§ë‡§´ ‡§á‡§Ç‡§°‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ) ‡§ï‡•á ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ß‡•ç‡§Ø‡§Æ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§°‡§æ‡§Ø‡§∞‡•á‡§ï‡•ç‡§ü ‡§¨‡•á‡§®‡§ø‡§´‡§ø‡§ü ‡§ü‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§Ç‡§∏‡§´‡§∞ (DBT) ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§≤‡§æ‡§≠ ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§™‡•ç‡§§ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è, ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§¨‡•à‡§Ç‡§ï ‡§ñ‡§æ‡§§‡•á ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§ß‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§®‡§Ç‡§¨‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§Ç‡§ï ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§µ‡§∂‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§ï‡•ç‡§∞‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ë‡§®‡§≤‡§æ‡§á‡§® ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§ë‡§´‡§≤‡§æ‡§á‡§® ‡§¶‡•ã‡§®‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§§‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ï‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ú‡§æ ‡§∏‡§ï‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§
üì¢ ‡§ë‡§®‡§≤‡§æ‡§á‡§® ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§ï‡•ç‡§∞‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ: ‡§á‡§Ç‡§ü‡§∞‡§®‡•á‡§ü ‡§¨‡•à‡§Ç‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ç‡§ó ‡§ï‡•á ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ß‡•ç‡§Ø‡§Æ ‡§∏‡•á:
  • NPCI ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ë‡§´‡§ø‡§∏‡§ø‡§Ø‡§≤ Website ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§Ø‡•á‡§Ç
  • "Consumer" ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§≤‡§ø‡§ï ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç
  • Bharat Aadhaar Seeding Enabler (BASE) ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§≤‡§ø‡§ï ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç ‡•§
  • Aadhaar Seeding/Deseeding ‡§ü‡•á‡§™ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§≤‡§ø‡§ï ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á
  • ‡§Ü‡§ß‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§ñ‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§¨‡§ß‡§ø‡§§ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§≠‡§∞‡§ï‡•á ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§∏‡§¨‡§Æ‡§ø‡§ü ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
  • (‡§Ö‡§•‡§µ‡§æ)
  • ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§¨‡•à‡§Ç‡§ï ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§á‡§Ç‡§ü‡§∞‡§®‡•á‡§ü ‡§¨‡•à‡§Ç‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ç‡§ó ‡§∏‡•á‡§µ‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§≤‡•â‡§ó‡§ø‡§® ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
  • '‡§Ü‡§ß‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•Ä‡§°‡§ø‡§Ç‡§ó' ‡§Ø‡§æ '‡§Ü‡§ß‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§≤‡§ø‡§Ç‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ç‡§ó' ‡§µ‡§ø‡§ï‡§≤‡•ç‡§™ ‡§ö‡•Å‡§®‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
  • ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§ß‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§®‡§Ç‡§¨‡§∞ ‡§¶‡§∞‡•ç‡§ú ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§µ‡§∂‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï ‡§µ‡§ø‡§µ‡§∞‡§£ ‡§≠‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
  • ‡§∏‡§¨‡§Æ‡§ø‡§ü ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§¨‡§æ‡§¶, ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•á ‡§™‡§Ç‡§ú‡•Ä‡§ï‡•É‡§§ ‡§Æ‡•ã‡§¨‡§æ‡§á‡§≤ ‡§®‡§Ç‡§¨‡§∞ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§è‡§ï ‡§ì‡§ü‡•Ä‡§™‡•Ä (OTP) ‡§Ü‡§è‡§ó‡§æ‡•§
  • ‡§ì‡§ü‡•Ä‡§™‡•Ä ‡§¶‡§∞‡•ç‡§ú ‡§ï‡§∞‡§ï‡•á ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§ï‡•ç‡§∞‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§™‡•Ç‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
üì¢ ‡§Æ‡•ã‡§¨‡§æ‡§á‡§≤ ‡§¨‡•à‡§Ç‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ç‡§ó ‡§ê‡§™ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ß‡•ç‡§Ø‡§Æ ‡§∏‡•á:
  • ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§¨‡•à‡§Ç‡§ï ‡§ï‡•á ‡§Ü‡§ß‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡§ø‡§ï ‡§Æ‡•ã‡§¨‡§æ‡§á‡§≤ ‡§ê‡§™ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§≤‡•â‡§ó‡§ø‡§® ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§

Promotion or Ads on Whatsapp Channel Terms
üîó ‚Ä¢ Terms & Conditions for WhatsApp Promotion

Terms & Conditions for WhatsApp Promotion

1. Posting Duration:

The post/link you provide will be shared on our channel for a fixed duration of 24-48 hours only.

2. Right to Update New Posts:

30 minutes after your post or link is shared, we reserve the right to update new posts on our channel.

3. Post Removal:

Once the specified duration ends, your post/link will be removed from our channel.

üîó ‚Ä¢ Apaar ID Card Download

Apaar ID Card Download

The APAAR ID card, also known as the One Nation One Student ID, is a unique 12-digit identification number for students in India. It's designed to digitally store and manage all academic credits, including scorecards, mark sheets, degrees, diplomas, and certificates.

  • ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡§æ ‡§Ö‡§™‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§à‡§°‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§° ‡§°‡§æ‡§â‡§®‡§≤‡•ã‡§° ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è, ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§Æ ‡§§‡•å‡§∞ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§á‡§® ‡§ö‡§∞‡§£‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§™‡§æ‡§≤‡§® ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§ó‡§æ:
  • ‡§Ü‡§ß‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡§ø‡§ï ‡§µ‡•á‡§¨‡§∏‡§æ‡§á‡§ü ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç: ‡§è‡§ï‡•á‡§°‡§Æ‡§ø‡§ï ‡§¨‡•à‡§Ç‡§ï ‡§ë‡§´ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§∞‡•á‡§°‡§ø‡§ü (ABC) ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§µ‡•á‡§¨‡§∏‡§æ‡§á‡§ü ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§ß‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡§ø‡§ï ‡§Ö‡§™‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§µ‡•á‡§¨‡§∏‡§æ‡§á‡§ü ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡•§
  • ‡§≤‡•â‡§ó ‡§á‡§® ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç: ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§≠‡§µ‡§§‡§É ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§°‡§ø‡§ú‡§ø‡§≤‡•â‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§∞‡•á‡§°‡•á‡§Ç‡§∂‡§ø‡§Ø‡§≤‡•ç‡§∏ ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ö‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§™‡§Ç‡§ú‡•Ä‡§ï‡•É‡§§ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§∞‡•á‡§°‡•á‡§Ç‡§∂‡§ø‡§Ø‡§≤‡•ç‡§∏ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§â‡§™‡§Ø‡•ã‡§ó ‡§ï‡§∞‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡•â‡§ó ‡§á‡§® ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§ó‡§æ‡•§

  • ‡§°‡§æ‡§â‡§®‡§≤‡•ã‡§° ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç: ‡§è‡§ï ‡§¨‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ú‡§¨ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§µ‡§ø‡§ï‡§≤‡•ç‡§™ ‡§¢‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§¢ ‡§≤‡•á‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡§æ ‡§Ö‡§™‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§à‡§°‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§° ‡§°‡§æ‡§â‡§®‡§≤‡•ã‡§° ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§ë‡§®-‡§∏‡•ç‡§ï‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä‡§® ‡§®‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§¶‡•á‡§∂‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§™‡§æ‡§≤‡§® ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§Ü‡§Æ‡§§‡•å‡§∞ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§™‡•Ä‡§°‡•Ä‡§è‡§´ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∞‡•Ç‡§™ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§â‡§™‡§≤‡§¨‡•ç‡§ß ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

1. ‡§≠‡§∞‡•ç‡§§‡•Ä ‡§™‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç (Recruitment Exams)

(a) ‡§ó‡•ç‡§∞‡•Å‡§™-1 ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§ó‡•ç‡§∞‡•Å‡§™-2 ‡§≠‡§∞‡•ç‡§§‡•Ä

  • ‡§â‡§¶‡§æ‡§π‡§∞‡§£: ‡§∏‡§π‡§æ‡§Ø‡§ï ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§¨‡§Ç‡§ß‡§ï, ‡§ï‡§®‡§ø‡§∑‡•ç‡§† ‡§Ö‡§≠‡§ø‡§Ø‡§Ç‡§§‡§æ, ‡§ó‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§Æ‡•Ä‡§£ ‡§µ‡§ø‡§∏‡•ç‡§§‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§Ö‡§ß‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä‡•§

(b) ‡§™‡§ü‡§µ‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§≠‡§∞‡•ç‡§§‡•Ä ‡§™‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§æ

  • ‡§ó‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§Æ‡•Ä‡§£ ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§∂‡§æ‡§∏‡§® ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§≠‡•Ç‡§Æ‡§ø ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§¨‡§Ç‡§ß‡§® ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ú‡•Å‡§°‡§º‡•á ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§∂‡•ç‡§® ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ‡•á ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§

(c) ‡§™‡•Å‡§≤‡§ø‡§∏ ‡§≠‡§∞‡•ç‡§§‡•Ä ‡§™‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§æ

  • ‡§™‡§¶: ‡§™‡•Å‡§≤‡§ø‡§∏ ‡§ï‡§æ‡§Ç‡§∏‡•ç‡§ü‡•á‡§¨‡§≤, ‡§∏‡§¨-‡§á‡§Ç‡§∏‡•ç‡§™‡•á‡§ï‡•ç‡§ü‡§∞ (SI), ‡§∞‡•á‡§°‡§ø‡§Ø‡•ã ‡§ë‡§™‡§∞‡•á‡§ü‡§∞, ‡§°‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§á‡§µ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§æ‡§Ç‡§∏‡•ç‡§ü‡•á‡§¨‡§≤‡•§
  • ‡§´‡§ø‡§ú‡§ø‡§ï‡§≤ ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§≤‡§ø‡§ñ‡§ø‡§§ ‡§™‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§æ ‡§∂‡§æ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§≤ ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§

(d) ‡§∂‡§ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§ï ‡§™‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡§§‡§æ ‡§™‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§æ (TET)

  • ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§•‡§Æ‡§ø‡§ï ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ß‡•ç‡§Ø‡§Æ‡§ø‡§ï ‡§∏‡•ç‡§§‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∂‡§ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§ï ‡§™‡§¶‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è‡•§

  • ‡§ï‡•É‡§∑‡§ø ‡§µ‡§ø‡§≠‡§æ‡§ó ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§§‡§ï‡§®‡•Ä‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§™‡§¶‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è‡•§

2. ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§µ‡•á‡§∂ ‡§™‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç (Entrance Exams)

(a) ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä-‡§è‡§ó‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ï‡§≤‡•ç‡§ö‡§∞ ‡§ü‡•á‡§∏‡•ç‡§ü (PAT)

  • ‡§ï‡•É‡§∑‡§ø ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§¨‡§Ç‡§ß‡§ø‡§§ ‡§™‡§æ‡§†‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§∞‡§Æ‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§µ‡•á‡§∂‡•§

(b) ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä-‡§®‡§∞‡•ç‡§∏‡§ø‡§Ç‡§ó ‡§ü‡•á‡§∏‡•ç‡§ü (PNT)

  • Application Begin : 01/01/2025
